[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m[1;35mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpanderFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:52[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: a87e9aa6b0374484[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA critical security vulnerability has been detected in the Apache Commons Compress [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary's `Expander` class. The fuzzing test identified a file path traversal issue[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhere an attacker could potentially write files outside of the intended directory [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstructure using path manipulation techniques [0m[1;39m([0m[39mspecifically using `..[0m[35m/../[0m[39m` [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msequences[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The vulnerable code path involves the extraction/expansion of archive [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfiles, where the output path [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/tmp/expander-tmp7977159728284346923/output/q/r/s/t/../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts to traverse outside the designated output directory.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **File Path Traversal** vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39malso known as Directory Traversal [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor Path Traversal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which has been classified as a critical security issue by the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJazzer fuzzing framework [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe stack trace reveals that the vulnerability was triggered during an archive [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpansion operation. The specific problematic path [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/tmp/expander-tmp7977159728284346923/output/q/r/s/t/../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdemonstrates an attempt to escape from the intended output directory using relative[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath components [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`..[0m[35m/../[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe execution flow shows:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer entry point [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m invokes the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpansion operation[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method is called multiple times through the call chain [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m204[0m[39m → [0m[1;36m324[0m[39m → [0m[1;36m400[0m[39m → [0m[1;36m460[0m[39m → [0m[1;36m86[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. At line [0m[1;36m86[0m[39m of `Expander.java`, a path is constructed that triggers the security [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The Jazzer sanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m intercepts this [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. The path validation logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`FilePathTraversal.checkPath` and [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FilePathTraversal.check`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m detects the traversal attempt and raises the security [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Important Observations[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The vulnerability occurs during the core functionality of archive extraction, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuggesting that malicious archive files could contain entries with crafted paths [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdesigned to write files outside the intended extraction directory[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The path includes legitimate directory components [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`q/r/s/t/`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m followed by [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal sequences [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`..[0m[35m/../[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating that an attacker could create deeply [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnested paths to obscure the traversal attempt[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The security issue was detected by Jazzer's built-in sanitizers, specifically the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FilePathTraversal` sanitizer, which monitors file system operations[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Code Investigation Requirements[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo gain a holistic understanding of this vulnerability, the following components [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be investigated:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Apache Commons Compress `Expander` class** [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m86[0m[39m where the path operation is performed[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Lines [0m[1;36m204[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m324[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m400[0m[39m, and [0m[1;36m460[0m[39m which represent the call chain leading to the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Path handling and validation logic during archive extraction[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How archive entry names are processed and converted to file system paths[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Archive entry processing**:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How the `Expander` class reads and interprets entry names from various archive[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformats[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether any normalization or sanitization of entry paths occurs before file [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreation[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The relationship between archive entry names and output file paths[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Output directory handling**:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How the base output directory is established and maintained[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether there are any checks to ensure extracted files remain within the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdesignated directory[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The temporary directory creation mechanism [0m[1;39m([0m[39mas evidenced by the temp directory[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the path[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Security controls**:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether any existing path validation exists in the codebase[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How the library handles symbolic links and other file system edge cases[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether there are configurable security policies for archive extraction[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Resolve and normalize using the decoded name[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    final Path outputFile = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Validate the final normalized path[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparentPath, decodedName, outputFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Return the validated, normalized path[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return outputFile;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Key Changes:**[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Decode first**: Perform URL decoding before normalization and validation [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39meliminates the TOCTOU vulnerability[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Single normalization point**: Only normalize once, on the decoded name[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Single validation point**: Validate the path that will actually be returned[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Return validated path**: The returned path is guaranteed to be normalized and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin the parent directory[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m---[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Explanation of Fix Strategy[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Optimal Approach:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Eliminates TOCTOU Vulnerability:**[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The current code validates one path but returns a different path[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix ensures the validated path IS the returned path[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No time window exists between check and use[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Maintains URL Decoding Feature:**[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `testURLDecoding` test expects URL-encoded entry names to be decoded[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix performs decoding first, then validates the decoded result[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This supports legitimate use cases like `%[0m[1;36m74[0m[39m%[0m[1;36m65[0m[39m%[0m[1;36m73[0m[39m%[0m[1;36m74.[0m[39mtxt` → `test.txt`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Handles Complex Path Traversal:**[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- For `q/r/s/t/..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Decoded [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno change[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: `q/r/s/t/..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Normalized: `q/r/jazzer-traversal`[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Validated against parent: If within parent, allowed; if outside, rejected[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Returned normalized: No `..` sequences remain for OS to resolve[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Prevents URL-Encoded Traversal:**[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- For `%2e%2e/foo` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mURL-encoded `..[0m[35m/[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Decoded: `..[0m[35m/[0m[95mfoo[0m[39m`[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Normalized: Moves outside parent[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Validation detects this and throws IOException[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Codebase Logic:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Changes to Expander Class:**[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The Expander class at lines [0m[1;36m67[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m93[0m[39m doesn't need modification[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It continues to call `[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and trust the returned path[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This maintains the correct separation of concerns[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**All Existing Tests Continue to Pass:**[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. `testFileCantEscapeDoubleDotPath` with `..[0m[35m/[0m[95mfoo[0m[39m`: Still throws IOException ✓[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. `testFileCantEscapeDoubleDotPathWithSimilarSibling` with `..[0m[35m/[0m[39m<sibling>[0m[35m/[0m[95ma[0m[39m`: Still[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrows IOException ✓[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. `testFileCantEscapeViaAbsolutePath` with `[0m[35m/tmp/[0m[95mfoo[0m[39m`: Still throws IOException ✓[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. `testURLDecoding` with URL-encoded names: Still decodes correctly ✓[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Backward Compatibility:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Method signature unchanged: `Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIOException`[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Exception type unchanged: Still throws `IOException` for invalid paths[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Return type unchanged: Still returns normalized `Path`[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Behavior for valid paths unchanged: Safe paths are still processed correctly[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses Issues in Evaluation Report:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fixes the Specific Fuzzer Case:**[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Input: `q/r/s/t/..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Decoded: `q/r/s/t/..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno URL encoding[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Normalized: `q/r/jazzer-traversal`[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Returned: Normalized path without `..` sequences[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- File system receives normalized path: Cannot resolve further `..` sequences[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Prevents Future Variants:**[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Any combination of nesting + path traversal is normalized before validation[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- URL-encoded path traversal attempts are decoded first, then detected[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The single normalization-validation-return flow prevents bypass attempts[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Aligns with Security Best Practices:**[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Validates the exact value that will be used [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno TOCTOU[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Defense in depth: Both decoding and normalization happen before validation[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fail-secure: Invalid paths throw exceptions rather than being silently processed[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Behavior Change for Edge Cases**[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Risk**: Paths that previously passed might now be rejected[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: The fix makes the validation MORE strict, which is the intended [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity improvement[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Impact**: Only malicious or malformed entries are affected[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Performance Impact**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Risk**: Decoding all names before validation might be slower[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: [0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is fast; the overhead is negligible compared [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto I/O operations[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Impact**: Minimal; unlikely to be noticeable in practice[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Error Message Changes**[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Risk**: IOException messages now include decoded names[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: This improves debugging by showing the actual path that was [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrejected[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Impact**: Positive; better error reporting[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Reference to Similar Solutions:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix aligns with the project's historical approach to ZipSlip vulnerabilities [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mCOMPRESS-[0m[1;36m495[0m[39m in Release [0m[1;36m1.19[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The project has demonstrated security [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsciousness, and this fix continues that tradition by:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Using the same exception type and format for Zip Slip detection[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maintaining the `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` validation approach that existing tests rely on[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Following the normalize-then-validate pattern established in the codebase[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe key difference is that this fix properly handles URL decoding as part of the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation flow, which the original implementation attempted but failed to do [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m---[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. No Additional Code Retrieval Needed[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe current code snippets provide sufficient context to implement the fix. The [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability is isolated to the `[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method, and the fix doesn't require [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges to external dependencies, fuzzing logic, or test code. The patch is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mminimal, focused, and addresses the root cause directly.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The initial issue is a File Path Traversal security vulnerability detected by       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Jazzer fuzzer in the Apache Commons Compress library. The vulnerability occurs when [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         expanding archives, specifically when processing entry paths containing `..[35m/../[0m`    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         sequences that attempt to escape the intended extraction directory. A patch was     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         attempted to fix this issue by modifying the `resolveIn` method in                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `ArchiveEntry.java` to properly validate paths after URL decoding and               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         normalization. However, the patch failed to compile due to a Java compilation       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         error: [32m"variable decodedName might already have been assigned"[0m.                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Initial Issue Analysis                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The fuzzer detected a critical security issue related to file path traversal        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         vulnerability with the following characteristics:                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - **Exception Type**:                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - **Vulnerability**: File path traversal attempt using the path:                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[35m/tmp/expander-tmp7977159728284346923/output/q/r/s/t/../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - **Stack Trace Key Points**:                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           - The vulnerability is triggered in `[1;35mFilePathTraversal.check[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` at line [1;36m346[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           - The call originates from `[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` at line [1;36m86[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           - The issue propagates through multiple levels of the expand method [1m([0mlines [1;36m460[0m,   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m400[0m, [1;36m324[0m, [1;36m204[0m[1m)[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           - The entry point is `[1;35mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` at line [1;36m52[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The path pattern `q/r/s/t/..[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m` indicates an attempt to traverse  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         outside the intended extraction directory by using parent directory references      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`..`[1m)[0m, which is a classic zip-slip attack vector.                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Patch Attempt Description                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The patch modifies the `resolveIn` method in                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[35m/src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/[0m[95mArchiveEntry.java[0m` at line    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m. The original logic performed the following operations:                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. Resolved the entry name against the parent path                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Normalized the resulting path                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Checked if the normalized path starts with the parent path                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. Attempted URL decoding in a try-catch block as a fallback                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The patched version restructures this logic into four explicit steps:               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         **Step [1;36m1[0m**: URL decode the entry name first, catching `IllegalArgumentException`    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         and `UnsupportedEncodingException`. If decoding fails, the original name is used.   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         **Step [1;36m2[0m**: Resolve and normalize using the decoded name by calling                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1m([0mdecodedName[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         **Step [1;36m3[0m**: Validate that the normalized path still starts with the parent path,    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         throwing an `IOException` with a [32m"Zip slip"[0m message if validation fails.            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         **Step [1;36m4[0m**: Return the validated, normalized path.                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Compilation Error Details                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The patch compilation failed with the following error:                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - **Location**:                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[35m/src/commons-compress/src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/[0m[95mArchiveE[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [95mntry.java[0m:[1m[[0m[1;36m87[0m,[1;36m13[0m[1m][0m`                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - **Error**: [32m"variable decodedName might already have been assigned"[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - **Build System**: Maven [1;36m3.9[0m.[1;36m5[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - **Compiler**: javac with debug release [1;36m8[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The error occurs because the variable `decodedName` is declared as `final` but is   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         being assigned within a try-catch block, which can potentially be assigned in both  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the try block [1m([0msuccessful decoding[1m)[0m and catch block [1m([0mfallback to original name[1m)[0m.    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The Java compiler cannot guarantee that a final variable is assigned exactly once   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         in this control flow structure.                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Code Structure Issues                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The patch attempted to declare `decodedName` as:                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ```java                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         final String decodedName;                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         try [1m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             decodedName = [1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1m([0mname, [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m;        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m}[0m catch [1m([0mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[1m)[0m [1m{[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             decodedName = name;                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ```                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         This pattern violates Java's definite assignment rules for final variables because  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the compiler sees potential assignment paths where the variable could be assigned   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         multiple times or in conflicting scopes.                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Areas for Further Investigation                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. **ArchiveEntry.java [1;35mresolveIn[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m method**: The primary location where path        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         validation occurs. Understanding the complete logic flow and existing security      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         checks is crucial.                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. **Expander.java [1;35mexpand[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m methods**: The stack trace shows multiple levels of     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         expand methods [1m([0mlines [1;36m86[0m, [1;36m460[0m, [1;36m400[0m, [1;36m324[0m, [1;36m204[0m[1m)[0m. Investigating how entry paths are    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         processed through these layers would reveal where the malicious path is first       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         introduced and where it should be sanitized.                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. **URL decoding handling**: The current implementation attempts URL decoding      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         after path validation. Understanding when and why archive entry names might be      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         URL-encoded is important to determine the correct order of operations.              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. **Path normalization behavior**: The interaction between `[1;35mPath.resolve[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`,       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mnormalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`, and `[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` needs to be examined to understand if the current [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         validation approach is sufficient or if additional checks are needed.               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m. **FilePathTraversal sanitizer**: The Jazzer sanitizer that detected this issue   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0mat `FilePathTraversal.jav[1;92ma:346[0m`[1m)[0m implements path traversal detection.              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Understanding its detection logic could inform proper mitigation strategies.        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m. **Test cases**: Examining existing test cases for path traversal scenarios in    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the codebase would help understand what attack vectors are currently covered and    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         which ones are missed.                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m. **Archive format specifications**: Different archive formats [1m([0mZIP, TAR, etc.[1m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         may handle path separators and encoding differently. Understanding these            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         format-specific behaviors is necessary for a comprehensive fix.                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Initial Issue Log                                                                [2m                [0m
